<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><img src="gy2eezjrrplq000001.jpg" title="" alt="" style="width:226px;height:64px;"></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;;font-size:18pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:18pt;letter-spacing:-0.4pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">LM Funding Reports Net Income of $4.4 Million or $0.87 Per Basic Common Share for the First Quarter of 2021</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">TAMPA, FL / ACCESSWIRE / May 14, 2021 /&#160;LM Funding America, Inc. (NASDAQ:LMFA) ("LM Funding" or "LMFA"),<font style="font-weight:normal;">&#160;a technology-based specialty finance company, today announced its financial results for the three months ended March 31, 2021.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Financial Highlights for the Three Month Period Ended March 31, 2021:</p>

<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">

<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font>Revenues declined to $177 thousand in 2021 from $341 thousand in Q1 2020.</p></td></tr></table></div>

(&#8216;Borqs&#8217;) initially projected to net $2 million.</p></td></tr></table></div>

<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font>Cash increased to $17.8 million on March 31, 2021 from $11.5 million on December 31, 2020.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#1D2228;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;Thus far in 2021 we continue to expand our &#8216;We Buy Problems&#8217; mission.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to $4.4 million in net income during the quarter, our cash position has increased to $17.8 million or $3.29 per basic common share as of March 31<sup style="font-size:85%;line-height:120%;vertical-align:top">st</sup>.&#8221;&nbsp;&nbsp;Said Bruce M. Rodgers, Chairman and CEO of LM Funding.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#8220;Revenues from our community association receivables business declined as we continue to develop a digital asset technology strategy to unlock the potential of this business.&nbsp;&nbsp;We expanded our core business of buying discounted debt and collecting it through court proceedings with the Borqs transaction.&nbsp;&nbsp;We entered the Borqs transaction projecting to net $2 million and we were pleased to realize a $5.7 million return. Going forward, we will continue to look for other technology enabled specialty finance business opportunities that can leverage our existing platform and expertise.&nbsp;&nbsp;We also expect our SPAC sponsorship and digital asset strategy to contribute to earnings in the foreseeable future as our core business navigates through the economy&#8217;s re-emergence from Covid restrictions.&#8221;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#1D2228;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Operational Highlights for the First Quarter of 2021 to Date:</p>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About LM Funding America:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">LM Funding America, Inc., together with its subsidiaries, is a technology-based specialty finance company that provides funding to nonprofit community associations (Associations) primarily located in the state of Florida, as well as in the states of Washington, Colorado and Illinois, by funding a certain portion of the associations' rights to delinquent accounts that are selected by the Associations arising from unpaid Association assessments.</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Forward-Looking Statements:</p>
<p style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">This press release may contain forward-looking statements made pursuant to the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Words such as &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; and &#8220;project&#8221; and other similar words and expressions are intended to signify forward-looking statements. Forward-looking statements are not guaranties of future results and conditions but rather are subject to various risks and uncertainties. Some of these risks and uncertainties are identified in the company's most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K and its other filings with the SEC, which are available at www.sec.gov. These risks and uncertainties include, without limitation, uncertainty created by the COVID-19 pandemic, our ability to acquire new accounts in our specialty finance business at appropriate prices, the need for capital, our ability to hire and retain new employees, changes in governmental regulations that affect our ability to collected sufficient amounts on defaulted consumer receivables, changes in the credit or capital markets, changes in interest rates, and negative press regarding the debt collection industry.&nbsp;&nbsp;The occurrence of any of these risks and uncertainties could have a material adverse effect on our business, financial condition, and results of operations.</p>
